msg:When traveling to Lingshui, Sanya, Hainan, choose a hotel in Haikou and take a stroll at Mangrove Bay. Note that the hotel is in Chengmai. First of all, Hilton's service is worthy of recognition. The hotel lobby is grand and there is a flamingo-themed afternoon tea. Check-in and check-out are very efficient. The biscuits provided at the front desk after check-in were delicious. Opening the balcony is the wetland park. The air is fresh and very eye-catching. The facilities and equipment in the room are complete, and the bedding and pajamas are good. The room hygiene is good. It looks fine at first glance. Meets five-star standards.
I also chose to have dinner at his Chinese restaurant. The set menu was cost-effective and delicious. The Wenchang chicken is smooth and tender, and the braised meat is fat but not greasy. The service is excellent.
There is a strange thing about their house. The water temperature in the bathtub is not as high as that in the shower. I don‚Äôt know if it‚Äôs because I washed it late or because of the special design. I personally feel that the water temperature in the bathtub is too low.
The Mangrove Bay Wetland Park next to the Hilton is pretty good. There are flamingos and you can hang crabsü¶Ä. The package we ordered included tickets, so it was a good deal.
I went to the Hilton for breakfast. It was very crowded, but the dishes were replenished very quickly, and the overall dishes were more Western-style. The taste is average, and there is a bread pudding that I really like.
Overall, the location of this hotel is actually a little bit out of the way. Although it is in the R&F Mangrove Bay Community, it is still a certain distance from the surrounding dining spots. However, I think hotel catering is okay. If you want to make a transition when traveling to Hainan, you might as well come to Chengmai Hilton.
